<script type="text/javascript">
       

        (function(global) {
            var extend = function(target, extendObj) {
                    for (var item in extendObj) {
                        if (extendObj.hasOwnProperty(item)) {
                            target[item] = extendObj[item];
                        }
                    }
                    return target;
                },
                sidebarConfig = extend({
                    activate: true
                }, global.SidebarConfig),
                scriptElm,
                loadScript = function(url, callback) {
                    var script = document.createElement("script");
                    script.type = "text/javascript";
                    if (script.readyState) { //IE
                        script.onreadystatechange = function() {
                            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                                script.readyState == "complete") {
                                script.onreadystatechange = null;
                                (callback && callback());
                            }
                        };
                    } else { //Others
                        script.onload = function() {
                            (callback && callback());
                        };
                    }
                    script.src = url;
                    document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
                };
            if(!global.SidebarConfig||!global.SidebarConfig.footerModules){
                global.SidebarConfig=global.SidebarConfig||{};
                global.SidebarConfig.footerModules=[{ name: 'koubei', layerClassName: 'layer chongqb-layer', layerCloseId:'' }, 'location', 'feedback', 'top'];
            }
            if (sidebarConfig.activate) {
                loadScript('http://js.inc.baa.bitautotech.com/c/c.js?s=quicklogin,Bitauto.iUtils,Bitauto.iMediator,ibt_userCars,Bitauto.Sidebar&v=1704011129');
            }
        })(window);
    </script>

function CheyishouDefaultSugKey() {
    var randomSugKey = "";
    var randomKey = randomSugKey.split(","),
        randomKeyIndex = Math.round(Math.random() * (randomKey.length - 1));
    var element = document.getElementById("sug_txtkeyword");
    element.value = randomKey[randomKeyIndex];
    //element.style.color = '#999';
}
